## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (ordinary differential equation rate laws)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is the time derivative of a concentration A, indicating an ODE-based kinetic model (rate law) for how a species concentration evolves in time. With only A and t available, plausible structures include mass-action orders in A, approach-to-equilibrium terms, autocatalysis/feedback, and explicitly time-varying effective rate coefficients.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant production/consumption rate limited by catalyst/flux)
- First-order decay/formation: dA_dt = c0 * A (unimolecular decay or growth under constant conditions)
- General n-th order (power-law) kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (effective reaction order c1 from mechanism/fit)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular self-reaction or approximation with other reactant constant)
- Approach to equilibrium (linear relaxation): dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (relaxation toward equilibrium concentration c1)
- Reversible/relaxation with nonlinear order: dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A**c2) (nonlinear restoring term; effective equilibrium in transformed variable)
- Autocatalytic (logistic-type) kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-enhancing growth with depletion/limitation)
- Generalized autocatalysis: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 * (c2 - A)**c3 (flexible autocatalysis and limitation exponents)
- Inhibition / saturating self-limitation: dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1) (rate increases with A but saturates due to inhibition/limited active sites)
- Substrate inhibition (decrease at high A): dA_dt = c0 * A / (A**2 + c1) (captures turnover drop at large A)
- Time-varying first-order rate coefficient: dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * A (slow drift in effective rate due to temperature/catalyst aging/feeding schedule)
- Periodic forcing of kinetics: dA_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (externally modulated rate via oscillatory conditions)
- Pulse/relaxation drive: dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) - c2 * A (time-dependent source with first-order removal)
- Mixed-order polynomial rate law: dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2 (empirical lumped kinetics when mechanism is unknown)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If dA_dt is approximately constant over wide A range → zero-order term c0 dominates (transport/catalyst-limited regime).
- If dA_dt vs A is approximately a straight line through the origin → first-order form c0 * A (unimolecular or pseudo-first-order).
- If plotting log(|dA_dt|) vs log(A) is linear → power-law order form c0 * A**c1 (effective reaction order from slope).
- If dA_dt changes sign at a specific A and is roughly proportional to (c1 - A) near that point → relaxation to equilibrium c0 * (c1 - A).
- If dA_dt is positive at intermediate A but near-zero at both small A and large A → autocatalytic limitation form c0 * A * (c1 - A) (S-shaped A(t)).
- If dA_dt increases with A at low A but plateaus at high A → saturating rational form c0 * A / (A + c1).
- If dA_dt increases with A at low A but decreases at high A (peaked rate curve) → substrate inhibition-like form c0 * A / (A**2 + c1) or c0 * A * (c1 - A).
- If residuals vs t show systematic drift after fitting an A-only rate law → include explicit time dependence in the coefficient, e.g., (c0 + c1 * t) * A.
- If dA_dt shows oscillatory patterns in time even at similar A → include periodic forcing in t, e.g., (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A.

Structure desc      : Additive model: A-linear baseline/log(t) plus an A-linear term multiplied by an exponential of a rational function of t. GT Equivalence Verification (CRK35)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_q*A*log(c2*t + c3)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is a fixed function of the form
\[
f(t,A)=A\Big(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)+\gamma\Big)
\]
with \(\alpha=0.062258070344434831\), \(\beta=0.9423435234237035\), \(\gamma=-0.13625696690019862\).
So any matching candidate must be **exactly linear in \(A\)**, have **only** a \(\log(\text{affine in }t)\) term (with +1 inside allowed), and a constant-in-\(t\) linear-in-\(A\) term; and it must have **no extra dependence** on \(A\) (like \(1/(A^2+c)\), \(\sqrt A\), \(\exp(A\cdot)\), \(\log(A\cdot)\), Max, Abs, etc.) and **no extra dependence** on \(t\) beyond the single log term.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether all extra terms can be eliminated by setting candidate constants to 0 (or otherwise), and whether the remaining structure can match \(A(c+\tilde c\log(\tilde\beta t+1))\).

---

### 1. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A c3\exp(c4/(c5+t))\)
Set \(c3=0\) to remove the exponential term. Remaining: \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)\), which matches GT by choosing \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\), \(c0=\gamma\). **Matches.**

### 2. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3/(A^2+c4)+A c5/(A^2+c6)\)
The rational terms depend on \(A\) nonlinearly; set \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\) to remove them. Remaining matches GT as in (1). **Matches.**

### 3. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{A c5} e^{c6 t}\)
GT has no additive constant independent of \(A\), so need \(c3=0\). Also GT has no exponential term, so set \(c4=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 4. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 t (A+c5)^{c6}\)
Need \(c3=0\) (no pure constant) and \(c4=0\) (no extra \(t\)/power term). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 5. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+c5\)
Need \(c5=0\) (no pure constant) and \(c2=0\) (remove exponential). Remaining \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) has **no** \(A\)-linear constant term \(\gamma A\). Cannot create \(\gamma A\) from the remaining structure. **No match.**

### 6. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3/(A^2+c4)+A c5/(A^2+c6)+A c7 e^{c8/(c9+t)}\)
Set \(c3=0,c5=0,c7=0\) to remove extra terms. Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 7. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 e^{A c4}\)
Set \(c3=0\) to remove exponential-in-\(A\) term. Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 8. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+A c5/(A+c6)+c7\)
Need \(c7=0\). Also must remove \(A c2 e^{...}\) and \(A c5/(A+c6)\) (non-GT forms): set \(c2=0,c5=0\). Remaining is \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) only, lacking \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 9. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3/(A^2+c4)+A c5/(A^2+c6)+c7\)
Need \(c7=0\). Set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 10. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{A c5 + c6 t}\)
Set \(c3=0\), \(c4=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 11. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A^{c3} c4 (A^{c3}+c5)^{c6}\)
Extra term is a nontrivial function of \(A\); set \(c4=0\) to remove it. Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 12. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+A c5(c6+t)^{c7}+c8\)
Need \(c8=0\). Remove extra terms by \(c2=0,c5=0\). Remaining \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) lacks \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 13. \(A c0 + A c1 + A c2\log(c3 t+1)+ c4 e^{c5 t}/A^{1/5}\)
The last term depends on \(A^{-1/5}\); must set \(c4=0\). Then expression becomes \(A(c0+c1)+A c2\log(c3 t+1)\), which matches GT by choosing \(c2=\alpha\), \(c3=\beta\), and \(c0+c1=\gamma\) (many solutions). **Matches.**

### 14. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{c5 t}\max(0,-A+c6)\)
Need \(c3=0\). The Max term introduces piecewise dependence on \(A\); must set \(c4=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 15. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+ c5 t/(c6 t+c7)+ c8/(c6 t+c7)+c9\)
GT has no terms independent of \(A\), so would need \(c5=c8=c9=0\). Also remove exponential by \(c2=0\). Remaining \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) lacks \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 16. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{A c5}e^{c6 t}+ c7 e^{A c8}e^{c9 t}\)
Set \(c3=0,c4=0,c7=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 17. Big rational expression with denominator \(A^2(A+c1)^5+c2(A+c1)^5=(A+c1)^5(A^2+c2)\)
This introduces complicated \(A\)-dependence unless all numerator coefficients except those reproducing \(A\) and \(A\log(\cdot)\) cancel the denominator. But the whole expression is of the form \(\frac{\text{poly in }A,t,\log}{(A+c1)^5(A^2+c2)}\), which cannot equal \(A(\gamma+\alpha\log(\beta t+1))\) for all \(A\) unless the denominator is constant (impossible) or the numerator contains the same factor to cancel it. The numerator terms have factors like \(A^3(A+c1)^5\), \(A(A+c1)^5\), etc., so cancellation of \((A+c1)^5\) is possible, but the remaining \(A^2+c2\) in denominator would still remain unless numerator also has factor \(A^2+c2\), which it does not (it’s linear combination of monomials, not multiplied by \(A^2+c2\)). Only way is to set all coefficients so the whole fraction is 0, but GT is not 0. **No match.**

### 18. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 e^{A c4}+ c5 e^{A c6 + c7\sin(c8 t+c9)}\)
Set \(c3=0,c5=0\) to remove exponentials. Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 19. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+A c5 e^{c6/(c7+t)}+c8\)
Need \(c8=0\). Remove exponentials by \(c2=0,c5=0\). Remaining lacks \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 20. \(\sqrt A c0 + A c1 + A c2\log(c3 t+1)+A c4 e^{c5 t}+ c6 e^{A c7}\)
Need no \(\sqrt A\): set \(c0=0\). No \(A e^{c5 t}\): set \(c4=0\). No \(e^{A c7}\): set \(c6=0\). Remaining \(A c1 + A c2\log(c3 t+1)\) matches GT with \(c1=\gamma,c2=\alpha,c3=\beta\). **Matches.**

### 21. \(\sqrt A c0 + \sqrt A c1 + A c2 + A c3\log(c4 t+1)+ c5 e^{c6 t}/A^{1/5}\)
Need remove \(\sqrt A\): \(c0=c1=0\). Remove \(A^{-1/5}\) term: \(c5=0\). Remaining \(A c2 + A c3\log(c4 t+1)\) matches GT with \(c2=\gamma,c3=\alpha,c4=\beta\). **Matches.**

### 22. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+A c5\log(c6 t+1)+c7\)
Need \(c7=0\), \(c2=0\). Then we have \(A[c0\log(c1 t+1)+c5\log(c6 t+1)]\): sum of two logs cannot equal \(\gamma+\alpha\log(\beta t+1)\) for all \(t\) unless one log term is zero and also we still lack \(\gamma A\). If set \(c5=0\), left with single log and still no \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 23. \(\sqrt A c0 + A c1 + A c2\log(c3 t+1)+ A + c4 e^{c5 t}/A^{1/5}\)
Set \(c0=0\), \(c4=0\). Remaining \(A(c1+1)+A c2\log(c3 t+1)\) matches GT with \(c2=\alpha,c3=\beta,c1+1=\gamma\). **Matches.**

### 24. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+c5 + c6 e^{c7/(c8+t)}\log(A c9+1)\)
Need remove \(c5\) (pure constant): set \(c5=0\). Remove exponential-log(A) term: set \(c6=0\). Remove \(A c2 e^{...}\): set \(c2=0\). Remaining is \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) lacking \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 25. Same issue as 24 but with \(\log(c9|A|+1)\); must set \(c6=0\), etc. Remaining lacks \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 26. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{A c5}e^{c6 t}+ c7 e^{c8 t}\log(A c9+1)\)
Set \(c3=0,c4=0,c7=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 27. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2 t+c3)+A c4 + A^{c5} c6 e^{c7 t}+ c8/(c2 t+c3)\)
To match GT, must remove reciprocal terms: set \(c1=0,c8=0\). Must remove \(A^{c5} e^{c7 t}\): set \(c6=0\). Remaining \(A(c0+c4)\) has no log term, so cannot match GT. **No match.**

### 28. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3/(A^2+c4)\)
Set \(c3=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 29. \(\sqrt A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A c3\log(c4 t+1)+ c5 e^{c6 t}\)
Need remove \(\sqrt A\): \(c0=0\). Remove pure \(e^{c6 t}\): set \(c5=0\). Remaining \(A(c1+c2)+A c3\log(c4 t+1)\) matches GT with \(c3=\alpha,c4=\beta,c1+c2=\gamma\). **Matches.**

### 30. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{c5 t}\log(A c6+1)\)
Need \(c3=0\). The \(\log(Ac6+1)\) term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 31. \(\sqrt A c0+\sqrt A c1 + A c2 + A c3 + A c4\log(c5 t+1)+ c6 e^{c7 t}/A^{1/5}\)
Set \(c0=c1=0\), \(c6=0\). Remaining \(A(c2+c3)+A c4\log(c5 t+1)\) matches GT. **Matches.**

### 32. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\)
Need \(c5=0\). Remove \(A e^{c4 t}\) term: set \(c3=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 33. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3 e^{A c4}e^{c5 t}+ c6 + c7 e^{A c8}e^{c9 t}\)
Need \(c6=0\). Remove exponentials: set \(c3=0,c7=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 34. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3 e^{c4/(c5+t)}+A c6\)
Remove exponential term by \(c3=0\). Then \(A(c0+c6)+A c1\log(c2 t+1)\) matches GT. **Matches.**

### 35. \(A c0\tanh(c1 t+c2)+ A c3/(c4+t)^{1/5}+ A + c5 e^{c6 t}+c7\)
To match GT must remove \(\tanh\), power, and \(e^{c6 t}\), and constants: set \(c0=0,c3=0,c5=0,c7=0\). Remaining is just \(A\), which cannot produce the log term. **No match.**

### 36. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3/(A^2+c4)+ A/(A^2+c5)\)
The last term \(A/(A^2+c5)\) cannot be removed by a coefficient (it has fixed coefficient 1). It is nonzero for generic \(A\), so cannot equal GT. **No match.**

### 37. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A^{c3} c4 e^{c5 t}+c6\)
Need \(c6=0\). Remove extra term by setting \(c4=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 38. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+c5 + c6 e^{c7 t}e^{c8/(c9+t)}\)
Need \(c5=0\). Also the last term is independent of \(A\); must set \(c6=0\). Remove exponential \(A c2 e^{...}\) by \(c2=0\). Remaining \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) lacks \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 39. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ c3 + c4 e^{c5 t}\)
Need \(c3=0\) and remove pure exponential by \(c4=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 40. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3 e^{c4/(c5+t)}+ c6 t/(A c7+c8)+ c9/(A c7+c8)\)
The last two terms introduce non-linear dependence on \(A\) unless \(c6=c9=0\). Set \(c6=0,c9=0\). Remove exponential by \(c3=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 41. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3 + A c4\log(c5 t+1)+ c6 + c7 e^{A c8}e^{c9 t}\)
Need \(c6=0\), remove exponential by \(c7=0\). Then we have two log terms; set \(c4=0\) to keep only one log. Remaining \(A(c0+c3)+A c1\log(c2 t+1)\) matches GT. **Matches.**

### 42. \(A^2 c0 e^{c1 t}+ A c2 + A c3 + A^{c4} c5 + A^{c6} c7 e^{c8 t}\)
GT is linear in \(A\) and has a log(t) term. This candidate has no log and includes powers \(A^2\), \(A^{c4}\), etc. You can zero out some terms (set \(c0=0,c5=0,c7=0\)) leaving \(A(c2+c3)\), still no log. **No match.**

### 43. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}+ A c5 e^{c6/(c7+t)}\log(c8 t+1)+c9\)
Need \(c9=0\). Remove exponential terms by \(c2=0,c5=0\). Remaining \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)\) lacks \(\gamma A\). **No match.**

### 44. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3 e^{c4 t}+ c5 + c6 e^{A c7}e^{c8 t}\)
Need \(c5=0\). Remove extra exponentials by \(c3=0,c6=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 45. \(\sqrt A c0 + A c1 + A c2 + A c3\log(c4 t+1)+ A c5 e^{c6 t}\)
Set \(c0=0\), remove \(A e^{c6 t}\) by \(c5=0\). Remaining matches GT with \(c1+c2=\gamma\), \(c3=\alpha\), \(c4=\beta\). **Matches.**

### 46. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A c3/(A^2+c4)+ A c5/(A^2+c6)+ A c7\)
Set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Then \(A(c0+c7)+A c1\log(c2 t+1)\) matches GT. **Matches.**

### 47. \(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t}/(A+c3)+ A^{c4} c5 + A^{c6} c7 e^{c8 t}\)
Has unavoidable non-linear \(A\) dependence unless \(c1=0,c5=0,c7=0\), leaving \(A c0\) only, no log. **No match.**

### 48. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2 t+c3)+ A^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t}+ c7/(c2 t+c3)\)
To remove reciprocal terms set \(c1=0,c7=0\). Remove power-exponential by \(c5=0\). Remaining \(A c0\) only, no log. **No match.**

### 49. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+ A^{c3} c4 e^{c5 t}+ c6 + c7 e^{A c8}e^{c9 t}\)
Need \(c6=0\). Remove extra terms by \(c4=0,c7=0\). Remaining matches GT. **Matches.**

### 50. \(A c0 + A c1/(c2 t+c3)+ c4 e^{c5 t}+ c6 + c7/(c2 t+c3)\)
Even if set \(c4=0,c6=0,c1=0,c7=0\), remaining is \(A c0\) with no log. Also original has no log form at all. **No match.**
